\def\lthtmlsetinline{\hbox{\vrule width.1em \vtop{\vbox{%
  \kern.1em\copy\sizebox}\ifdim\dp\sizebox>0pt\kern.1em\else\kern.3pt\fi
  \ifdim\hsize>\wd\sizebox \hrule depth1pt\fi}}}
\def\lthtmlsetmath{\hbox{\vrule width.1em\kern-.05em\vtop{\vbox{%
  \kern.1em\kern0.8 pt\hbox{\hglue.17em\copy\sizebox\hglue0.8 pt}}\kern.3pt%
  \ifdim\dp\sizebox>0pt\kern.1em\fi \kern0.8 pt%
  \ifdim\hsize>\wd\sizebox \hrule depth1pt\fi}}}
\def\centerinlinemath{%
  \dimen1=\ifdim\ht\sizebox<\dp\sizebox \dp\sizebox\else\ht\sizebox\fi
  \advance\dimen1by.5pt \vrule width0pt height\dimen1 depth\dimen1 
 \dp\sizebox=\dimen1\ht\sizebox=\dimen1\relax}

$\displaystyle \sum_{i=1}^j q^{-i}x_{k i}x_{l i'}\wr \beta = 
\sum_{i=1}^j q^{i-2j}x_{k i'}x_{l i}.
$%
\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath20643}%
\begin{displaymath}
\begin{array}{rcl}
\sum_{i=1}^{j} q^{-i}x_{k i} x_{l i'}\wr \beta & = &
\sum_{i=1}^{j} (q^{-i}x_{k i'} x_{l i} -(y-1)\sum_{h=1}^{i-1}
y^{-i}q^hx_{k h'} x_{l h}) \\
& = & 
\sum_{i=1}^{j} q^{-i+2}x_{k i'} x_{l i} -
(y-1)\sum_{1 \geq h\geq i \geq j}
y^{-i}q^hx_{k h'} x_{l h} \\
\end{array}
\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\\
& = & 
\sum_{i=1}^m q^{-i}x_{k i}x_{l i'}-q^{i-2(m+1)}x_{k i'}x_{l i} \\
& = &

$ \mapsto$%

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_indisplay24347}%
$\displaystyle v_{i}v_{j}v_{k} \mapsto -q^{{\rm sign}(j-i)}v_{j}v_{i}v_{k} 
\mapsto q^{{\rm sign}(j-i)+{\rm sign}(k-i)} v_{j}v_{k}v_{i}
\mapsto -q^{{\rm sign}(j-i)+{\rm sign}(k-i)+{\rm sign}(k-j)}v_{k}v_{j}v_{i}, 
$%
\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_indisplay24349}%
$\displaystyle v_{i}v_{j}v_{k} \mapsto -q^{{\rm sign}(k-j)}v_{i}v_{k}v_{j}
\mapsto q^{{\rm sign}(k-i)+{\rm sign}(k-j)} v_{k}v_{i}v_{j}
\mapsto -q^{{\rm sign}(j-i)+{\rm sign}(k-i)+{\rm sign}(k-j)}v_{k}v_{j}v_{i}. 
$%
\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath24351}%
\begin{displaymath}
\begin{array}{lll}
v_{i'}v_{i}v_{i} & 
\mapsto & -q^{-2}v_{i}v_{i'}v_{i}
-(q^{-2}-1)\sum_{j=i+1}^mq^{i-j}v_{j}v_{j'}v_{i} \\
& \mapsto & -q^{-2}( -q^{-2}v_{i'}v_{i}v_{i}
-(q^{-2}-1)\sum_{j=i+1}^mq^{i-j}v_{i}v_{j}v_{j'})\\
& &-(q^{-2}-1)\sum_{j=i+1}^mq^{i-j + {\rm sign}(i-j')}v_{j}v_{i}v_{j'}\\
& \mapsto & q^{-2}(q^{-2}-1)\sum_{j=i+1}^mq^{i-j}v_{i}v_{j}v_{j'})\\
& & -q^{{\rm sign}(i-j')+{\rm sign}(i-j)}(q^{-2}-1)\sum_{j=i+1}^mq^{i-j}v_{i}v_{j}v_{j'}
=0.
\end{array}
\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsection}
{\newpage\clearpage

$ \beta(c_i)$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline24394}%
$ \beta(d_i)$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath24396}%
\begin{displaymath}
\begin{array}{rcl}
\beta(c_i) & = & q^i\beta( v_{i'}v_{i}) \\
& = & q^i(v_{i}v_{i'}+(y-1)v_{i'}v_{i}
-(y-1)\sum_{k=i+1}^nq^{\rho_k-\rho_i}\epsilon_k\epsilon_iv_{k}v_{k'} ) \\
& = & -y^i d_i+(y-1)c_i
-(y-1)q^i(\sum_{k=i+1}^mq^{i-k}v_{k}v_{k'}+ 
\sum_{k=1}^m-q^{-\rho_k -\rho_i}v_{k'}v_{k} ) \\
& = & -y^id_i+(y-1)(c_i +
y^i(\sum_{k=i+1}^m d_k + y^{-m-1} 
\sum_{k=1}^m c_k ) )\\\\
\beta(d_i) & = & -q^{-i}\beta( v_{i}v_{i'}) \\
& = & -q^{-i}(v_{i'}v_{i}
-(y-1)\sum_{k=i'+1}^nq^{\rho_k-\rho_i}\epsilon_k\epsilon_{i'}v_{k}v_{k'} ) \\
& = & -y^{-i} c_i+
(y-1)q^{-i}\sum_{k=1}^{i-1}q^{\rho_{k'}-\rho_{i'}}v_{k'}v_{k} \\
& = & -y^{-i} c_i+
(y-1)y^{-i}\sum_{k=1}^{i-1}c_k
\end{array}
\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline24398}%
$ \beta(y^{-i}c_i-y^{-1}d_i-(y^{-1}-1)\sum_{j=i+1}^md_j)=$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath24400}%
\begin{displaymath}
\begin{array}{rcl}
& - & d_i+y^{-i}(y-1)c_i+(y-1)(\sum_{k=i+1}^md_k + y^{-m-1}\sum_{k=1}^m c_k)\\
& + &  y^{-i-1} c_i + y^{-i}(y^{-1}-1)\sum_{k=1}^{i-1}c_k \\
& - &  (y^{-1}-1)\sum_{j=i+1}^{m}( -y^{-j}c_j + y^{-j}(y-1) \sum_{k=1}^{j-1} c_k )
\end{array}
\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath24402}%
\begin{displaymath}
\begin{array}{rcl}
 \sum_{j=i+1}^{m}( -y^{-j}c_j + y^{-j}(y-1) \sum_{k=1}^{j-1} c_k ) & = &
- \sum_{k=i+1}^{m}y^{-k}c_k - (y-1) \sum_{j=i+1}^m\sum_{k=1}^{j-1} y^{-j}c_k 
\end{array}
\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath24404}%
\begin{displaymath}
\begin{array}{rcl}
\sum_{j=i+1}^m\sum_{k=1}^{j-1} y^{-j}c_k & = & 
\sum_{j=i+1}^m(\sum_{k=1}^{i-1} y^{-j}c_k + \sum_{k=i}^{j-1} y^{-j}c_k) \\
& = & \sum_{k=1}^{i-1}(\sum_{j=i+1}^my^{-j})c_k +
\sum_{k=i}^{m-1}(\sum_{j=k+1}^m y^{-j})c_k
\end{array}
\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage

\begin{array}{rcl}

\sum_{k=i}^{m-1}y^{-k}c_k -y^{-m}\sum_{k=1}^{m-1} c_k +y^{-i}\sum_{k=i}^{i-1}
c_k \\
& = & \sum_{k=i}^{m}y^{-k}c_k -y^{-m}\sum_{k=1}^{m} c_k +y^{-i}\sum_{k=i}^{i-1} c_k
\end{array}
\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

-y^{-m}c_m$%
